2.1.1.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-debug/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-debug/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:dtsrouter-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-debug/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-debug/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.DtsrouterDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_DtsrouterDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__DtsrouterDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.3.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-notice/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-notice/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:dtsrouter-notice/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-notice/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-notice/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.DtsrouterNotice.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_DtsrouterNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__DtsrouterNotice__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterNotice_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.6.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-critical/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-critical/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:dtsrouter-critical/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-critical/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-critical/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.DtsrouterCritical.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_DtsrouterCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__DtsrouterCritical__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterCritical_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.8.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-emergency/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-emergency/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:dtsrouter-emergency/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-emergency/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:dtsrouter-emergency/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.DtsrouterEmergency.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_DtsrouterEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__DtsrouterEmergency__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_DtsrouterEmergency_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.11.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:msg-end/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:msg-end/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:msg-end/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:msg-end/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:msg-end/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.MsgEnd.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_MsgEnd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__MsgEnd__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_MsgEnd_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.13.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:msg-flush/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:msg-flush/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:msg-flush/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:msg-flush/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:msg-flush/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.MsgFlush.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_MsgFlush_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__MsgFlush__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_MsgFlush_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_MsgFlush_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_MsgFlush_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.16.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:shared-registration/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:shared-registration/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:shared-registration/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:shared-registration/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:shared-registration/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.SharedRegistration.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_SharedRegistration_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__SharedRegistration__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.18.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:router-state-init/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:router-state-init/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:router-state-init/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:router-state-init/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:router-state-init/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.RouterStateInit.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_RouterStateInit_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__RouterStateInit__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_RouterStateInit_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_RouterStateInit_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_RouterStateInit_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.21.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:no-query-rsp-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:no-query-rsp-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:no-query-rsp-member/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:no-query-rsp-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:no-query-rsp-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.NoQueryRspMember.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_NoQueryRspMember_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__NoQueryRspMember__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.23.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:unexpected-query-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:unexpected-query-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:unexpected-query-result/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:unexpected-query-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:unexpected-query-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.UnexpectedQueryResult.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_UnexpectedQueryResult_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__UnexpectedQueryResult__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_UnexpectedQueryResult_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_UnexpectedQueryResult_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_UnexpectedQueryResult_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.25.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:query-result-ack/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:query-result-ack/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:query-result-ack/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:query-result-ack/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:query-result-ack/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.QueryResultAck.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_QueryResultAck_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__QueryResultAck__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_QueryResultAck_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_QueryResultAck_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier

    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use

2.1.28.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:query-result-error/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:query-result-error/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:query-result-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:query-result-error/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:query-result-error/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.QueryResultError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_QueryResultError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__QueryResultError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.30.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-evt-rsp-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-evt-rsp-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:xact-evt-rsp-member/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-evt-rsp-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-evt-rsp-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.XactEvtRspMember.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_XactEvtRspMember_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__XactEvtRspMember__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactEvtRspMember_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactEvtRspMember_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactEvtRspMember_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.32.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:member-bounce/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:member-bounce/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:member-bounce/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:member-bounce/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:member-bounce/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.MemberBounce.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_MemberBounce_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__MemberBounce__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_MemberBounce_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_MemberBounce_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier

    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of

2.1.35.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:brute-force-found/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:brute-force-found/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier

2.1.37.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:uncorrelated-query-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:uncorrelated-query-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:uncorrelated-query-result/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:uncorrelated-query-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:uncorrelated-query-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.UncorrelatedQueryResult.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_UncorrelatedQueryResult_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__UncorrelatedQueryResult__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.39.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:uncorrelated-empty-xact-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:uncorrelated-empty-xact-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:uncorrelated-empty-xact-result/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:uncorrelated-empty-xact-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:uncorrelated-empty-xact-result/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.UncorrelatedEmptyXactResult.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_UncorrelatedEmptyXactResult_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.41.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-send-msg/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-send-msg/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:xact-send-msg/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-send-msg/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-send-msg/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.XactSendMsg.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_XactSendMsg_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__XactSendMsg__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.44.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-info/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-info/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:xact-info/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-info/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-info/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.XactInfo.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_XactInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__XactInfo__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactInfo_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.46.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-summary/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-summary/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:xact-summary/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-summary/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-summary/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.XactSummary.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_XactSummary_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__XactSummary__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactSummary_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactSummary_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactSummary_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-filtered-member/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path

2.1.49.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:non-owner-xact-end-attempt/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:non-owner-xact-end-attempt/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:non-owner-xact-end-attempt/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:non-owner-xact-end-attempt/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:non-owner-xact-end-attempt/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier

2.1.51.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:peer-reg-failure/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:peer-reg-failure/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:peer-reg-failure/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:peer-reg-failure/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:peer-reg-failure/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.PeerRegFailure.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_PeerRegFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__PeerRegFailure__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_PeerRegFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_PeerRegFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_PeerRegFailure_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.53.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-dump-timeout/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:xact-dump-timeout/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:xact-dump-timeout/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-dump-timeout/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:xact-dump-timeout/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.XactDumpTimeout.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_XactDumpTimeout_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__XactDumpTimeout__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactDumpTimeout_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactDumpTimeout_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_XactDumpTimeout_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.56.1.3  container rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:notify-xact-query-error/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /rwdtsrouterlog:notify-xact-query-error/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /rw-dts-router-log:notify-xact-query-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:notify-xact-query-error/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/rwdtsrouterlog:notify-xact-query-error/rwdtsrouterlog:template_params/rwdtsrouterlog:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .rw_dts_router_log.YangNotif.RwDtsRouterLog.NotifyXactQueryError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    RwDtsRouterLogYang.YangNotif_RwDtsRouterLog_NotifyXactQueryError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    RwDtsRouterLog__YangNotif__RwDtsRouterLog__NotifyXactQueryError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    RwDtsRouterLog_RwDtsRouterLog_notif_NotifyXactQueryError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    RwDtsRouterLog_notif_NotifyXactQueryError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
